Simple non-colorful label with green tones (common color for Caudalie products since the brand focuses on skincare with grape extract).\n\n- Caudalie introduces this mineral spray as:\n + Containing 100% grape water and enriched with Polysaccharide (a natural moisturizing agent in skin that helps retain water and has high antioxidant properties - source: Paula\u2019s Choice) and mineral salts.\n + 100% extract directly from small grapes during harvest season, has a soothing, cooling and moisturizing effect on skin.\n\n - The product does not contain: Parabens, Sulfates and Phthalates.\n\n- Impressions: As I described at the beginning, mineral sprays don't have anything too flashy for me since their simple function is to provide extra hydration for the skin conveniently. I feel I like this Caudalie Grape Water spray more than other types because the grape extract makes me immediately think of the antioxidant effect for skin that grapes provide. Just from spraying I feel at least this type of water has some added superior effects over others (even if it doesn't contain 100% grape extract >.<) When spraying it feels like a fine mist, it's hard to detect the grape scent but in comparison with Avene, I can feel Caudalie Grape Water is slightly more refreshing (or maybe I'm too swayed by the \"100% extract from grapes\" claim ^^ ) The water droplets spray a little \"stronger\" than the Avene bottle but still super gentle on skin. Absorption is quite fast (almost instant) leaving skin feeling much more \"moist\". Some ways to use this mineral spray (you can definitely apply these to other mineral sprays too):\n\n + You can spray after cleansing and before applying moisturizer. A bit of water on skin will help the moisturizer absorb better (similar to cleansing but not using a towel to pat dry, just let skin air dry).\n + Spray after makeup application for a more natural makeup look.\n + Spray...anytime when you feel your skin needs extra hydration during the day (when you're a bit sleepy, spray onto skin for an instant refresh when you have to work or study too much).\n\nBasically I think this product meets the brand's claims. Like other mineral sprays, I don't notice any dramatic changes to my skin but using mineral spray (especially with grape extract) makes me feel like my skin is better cared for and instantly hydrated after a few sprays. (Theo m\u00ecnh quan s\u00e1t, nhi\u1ec1u ng\u01b0\u1eddi c\u00f3 suy ngh\u0129 \u201cti\u1ec1n b\u1ea1c l\u00e0 ngu\u1ed3n g\u1ed1c c\u1ee7a t\u1ed9i l\u1ed7i\u201d, \u201cnhi\u1ec1u ng\u01b0\u1eddi c\u00f3 ti\u1ec1n, nh\u01b0ng kh\u00f4ng h\u1ea1nh ph\u00fac \u21d2 m\u1ea5t n\u00e0y \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c kia\u201d, v\u1edbi m\u00ecnh ti\u1ec1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 mang \u0111\u1ebfn s\u1ef1 sung t\u00fac v\u00e0 h\u1ea1nh ph\u00fac th\u00ec t\u1ea1i sao m\u00ecnh l\u1ea1i kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 c\u1ea3 hai. N\u1ebfu b\u1ea1n mu\u1ed1n m\u00ecnh chia s\u1ebb nhi\u1ec1u h\u01a1n v\u1ec1 quan \u0111i\u1ec3m n\u00e0y th\u00ec h\u00e3y cmt cho m\u00ecnh bi\u1ebft nha.
